class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">npm Install Note: Hidden <code>.kilo</code> File</h3><a id=\"user-content-npm-install-note-hidden-kilo-file\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: npm Install Note: Hidden .kilo File\" href=\"#npm-install-note-hidden-kilo-file\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">On some systems and npm versions, installing <code>@kilocode/cli</code> can create a hidden <code>.kilo</code> file near the installed <code>kilo</code> command (for example in a global npm bin directory). This file is an npm-generated launcher helper, not project data.</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Why it exists: npm may create helper artifacts while wiring CLI executables.</li>\n<li>Size caveat: size can vary by platform, npm version, and install mode (symlink vs copied launcher), so a strict fixed size is not guaranteed.</li>\n<li>Safety: it is safe to leave in place. Do not edit it manually. Use your package manager's uninstall (<code>npm uninstall -g @kilocode/cli</code>) to remove install artifacts cleanly.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Install from GitHub Releases (Optional)</h3><a id=\"user-content-install-from-github-releases-optional\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Install from GitHub Releases (Optional)\" href=\"#install-from-github-releases-optional\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Download the latest binary or source code from the <a href=\"https://github.com/Kilo-Org/kilocode/releases\">Releases page</a>, use this quick guide:</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><code>kilo-&lt;os&gt;-&lt;arch&gt;.zip</code> is the CLI binary for your OS and CPU architecture on Windows and macOS. (<code>kilo-linux-&lt;arch&gt;.tar.gz</code> for Linux)</li>\n<li><code>darwin</code> means macOS.</li>\n<li><code>x64</code> is standard 64-bit Intel/AMD CPUs.</li>\n<li><code>x64-baseline</code> is a compatibility build for older x64 CPUs(do not support AVX Instruction).</li>\n<li><code>arm64</code> is ARM-based Linux/MacOS.</li>\n<li><code>musl</code> is statically linked Linux build for Alpine/minimal Docker without glibc. Alpine/minimal Docker users should prefer the matching *-musl asset.</li>\n<li><code>kilo-vscode-*.vsix</code> is the VS Code extension package and not the CLI binary.</li>\n<li><code>Source code</code> releases are for building from source, not normal installation.</li>\n</ul>\n<p dir=\"auto\">For most users:</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><strong>Windows (most PCs):</strong> <code>kilo-windows-x64.zip</code></li>\n<li><strong>macOS Apple Silicon:</strong> <code>kilo-darwin-arm64.zip</code></li>\n<li><strong>macOS Intel:</strong> <code>kilo-darwin-x64.zip</code></li>\n<li><strong>Linux x64:</strong> <code>kilo-linux-x64.tar.gz</code></li>\n<li><strong>Linux on ARM:</strong> <code>kilo-linux-arm64.tar.gz</code></li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Autonomous Mode (CI/CD)</h3><a id=\"user-content-autonomous-mode-cicd\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Autonomous Mode (CI/CD)\" href=\"#autonomous-mode-cicd\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Use the <code>--auto</code> flag with <code>kilo run</code> to enable fully autonomous operation without user interaction. This is ideal for CI/CD pipelines and automated workflows:</p>\n<div class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\"><pre>kilo run --auto <span
